# <a name="office-365-operated-by-21vianet"></a><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-104">由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-104">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-p102">由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365，是設計用以滿足在中國對於安全性、可靠性和可調整性雲端服務的需求。這項服務由 Microsoft 授權給 21Vianet 的技術提供支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-p102">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet is designed to meet the needs for secure, reliable, and scalable cloud services in China. This service is powered by technology that Microsoft has licensed to 21Vianet.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-107">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-107">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-108">Microsoft 不直接營運此項服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-108">Microsoft does not operate the service itself.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-109">由 21Vianet 營運、提供並管理服務的提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-109">21Vianet operates, provides, and manages delivery of the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-110">世紀是中國最大的電信型網際網路資料中心服務提供者，提供主控、managed 網路服務和雲端計算基礎結構服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-110">21Vianet is the largest carrier-neutral internet data center services provider in China, providing hosting, managed network services, and cloud computing infrastructure services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-111">使用 Microsoft 技術授權，世紀可運作本機 Office 365 資料中心，以提供使用 Office 365 服務的能力，同時保留中國內的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-111">By licensing Microsoft technologies, 21Vianet operates local Office 365 data centers to provide the ability to use Office 365 services while keeping data within China.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-112">21Vianet 也提供[訂閱和計費服務以及支援](/Office365/Admin/contact-support-for-business-products?preserve-view=true&tabs=phone&view=o365-21vianet)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-112">21Vianet also provides [subscription and billing services, as well as support](/Office365/Admin/contact-support-for-business-products?preserve-view=true&tabs=phone&view=o365-21vianet).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-113">這些服務須遵守中國法律。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-113">These services are subject to Chinese laws.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-114">由於中國服務的獨特性質（由中國內資料中心的合作夥伴運作），還有一些尚未啟用的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-114">Due to the unique nature of the China services—operated by a partner from data centers inside China—there are some features that have not yet been enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-115">經過一段時間後，客戶將會看到服務的功能逐漸完整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-115">Customers will see the services come closer to full feature parity over time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-116">有關的差異，請參閱服務描述註腳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-116">See the service description footnotes for differences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-117">如需更高層級的差異概觀，請參閱[深入了解由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365](/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-117">For a higher-level overview of differences, see [Learn about Office 365 operated by 21Vianet](/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china).</span></span>

## <a name="service-availability-within-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-118">每個方案中可用的服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-118">Service availability within each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-p105">每個由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 方案皆包含一些個別服務，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。下表顯示每項 Office 365 方案中可用的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-p105">Each Office 365 plan operated by 21Vianet includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online. The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>

## <a name="security-amp-compliance-center-availability-in-office-365-operated-by-21vianet"></a><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-236">Security &amp; Compliance Center availability in Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-236">Security &amp; Compliance Center availability in Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-237">Microsoft 365 規範中心可讓您輕鬆地存取所需的工具，以管理組織的合規性需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-237">Microsoft 365 Compliance Center provides easy access to the tools you need to manage your organization's compliance needs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-238">以下是由世紀運作的計畫提供的相容性中心的解決方案：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-238">The following solutions are available in Compliance Center for plans operated by 21Vianet:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-239">資料外洩防護 (DLP)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-239">Data Loss Prevention (DLP)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-240">保留</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-240">Retention</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-241">使用 Azure Active Directory 和 Exchange 中的資料進行審核</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-241">Auditing with data from Azure Active Directory and Exchange</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-242">Microsoft 資訊保護 (使用 AIP 整合標籤用戶端的 Office 用戶端和 Outlook 的 MIP) 和敏感度標籤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-242">Microsoft Information Protection (MIP) and sensitivity labels for Office clients and Outlook using the AIP unified label client</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-243">目前不支援在 SharePoint 網站、Microsoft 365 群組和 Microsoft 小組中保護內容的靈敏度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-243">Sensitivity labels to protect content in SharePoint sites, Microsoft 365 groups, and Microsoft Teams are not supported at this time.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-244">目前不支援使用網頁上的 Office 來分類及保護檔和電子郵件的靈敏度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-244">Sensitivity labels to classify and protect documents and emails with Office on the web are not supported at this time.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1207"><sup>14</sup> Outlook mobile (IOS 和 Android) 目前不支援多重要素驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1207"><sup>14</sup> Multi-factor authentication is not currently supported in Outlook mobile (iOS and Android).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1208"><sup>15</sup> OneNote 的類別筆記本是透過世紀提供，但是 OneNote 的類別筆記本工具列不適用於 Windows 10 應用程式、iPad 或網頁 OneNote。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1208"><sup>15</sup> OneNote Class Notebook is available via 21Vianet, but the OneNote Class Notebook toolbar is not available for Windows 10 apps, iPad, or OneNote for the web.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1209">由世紀運作的<sup>16</sup>位 Office 365 只支援保留原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1209"><sup>16</sup> Office 365 operated by 21Vianet only supports Retention policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1210">不支援 Yammer 及小組位置的保留標籤或保留原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1210">Retention labels or Retention policies for Yammer and Teams locations are not supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1211">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [使用保留原則快速入門](/microsoft-365/compliance/get-started-with-retention)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1211">For more details, see [Get started with retention policies](/microsoft-365/compliance/get-started-with-retention).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1212"><sup>17</sup> 在 microsoft 365 中的審計可讓組織深入瞭解 microsoft 365 中的不同服務所進行的各種審核活動類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1212"><sup>17</sup> Audit in Microsoft 365 provides organizations with visibility into many types of audited activities across different services in Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1213">使用 [安全性與 &amp; 合規性中心](./office-365-securitycompliance-center.md) 審核記錄搜尋，以查看組織中的使用者和系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1213">Use the [Security &amp; Compliance Center](./office-365-securitycompliance-center.md) audit log search to view user and administrator activity in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1214">您也可以使用 [Office 365 管理活動 API](/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference) ，從統一的審計記錄檔中取得事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1214">You can also use the [Office 365 Management Activity API](/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference) to retrieve events from the unified audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1215">當使用者或系統管理員執行已審核的活動時，會產生一個審計記錄，並將其儲存在客戶組織的審計記錄檔中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1215">When an audited activity is performed by a user or admin, an audit record is generated and stored in the audit log for the customer organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1216">在審核記錄) 中，保留審計記錄的時間長度 (及可供搜尋，取決於客戶的 Office 365 或 Microsoft 365 企業版訂閱，以及指派給特定使用者的授權類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1216">The length of time that an audit record is retained (and searchable in the audit log) depends on the customer's Office 365 or Microsoft 365 Enterprise subscription and the type of the license assigned to specific users.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1793"><sup>1</sup> 此版本的 Office 支援封存和相容性功能，但不包含 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online 方案，且必須另外購買或搭配支援的同等內部部署伺服器使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1793"><sup>1</sup> Archiving and compliance features are supported with this version of Office, but the Exchange Online and SharePoint Online plans are not included and must be purchased separately or used with supported on-premises server equivalents.</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1808"><sup>8</sup>Office 365 Enterprise E3 和 Office 365 專業增強版 的大量啟用僅限於在 Windows Server 2008 R2 與更新版本上的安裝，且須啟用 RDS 角色或 Windows To Go 安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1808"><sup>8</sup> Volume activation for Office 365 Enterprise E3 and Office 365 ProPlus are limited to installations on Windows Server 2008 R2 and newer with the RDS role enabled or Windows To Go installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1809">無論哪種情況，存取這些安裝的使用者都必須為 Office 365 Enterprise E3 或 Office 365 專業增強版 的授權使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1809">In either case, users accessing these installations need to be licensed users of Office 365 Enterprise E3 or Office 365 ProPlus.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1810"><sup>9</sup> 如果您在目前通道或已設定目標發行的順延通道上，則目前可以使用 Access。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1810"><sup>9</sup> Access is currently available if you're on Current Channel or on Targeted release for Deferred Channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1811">如果您在順延通道上，則可在 2017 年 6 月存取 Access。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1811">If you're on Deferred Channel, Access will be available in June 2017.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1812">如需詳細資訊，請參閱＜ [Office 365 商務版和商務進階版中將包含 Access](https://support.office.com/article/f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef)＞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1812">For more information, see [Access included as part of Office 365 Business and Business Premium](https://support.office.com/article/f55c8362-5816-4f8b-897d-0a05e7ba0fef).</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1813"><sup>10</sup> 目前在由世紀運作的 Office 365 預覽中使用的 web Visio。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1813"><sup>10</sup> Visio for the web is currently in preview for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1814">如需有關 web Visio 的詳細資訊，請參閱 [visio for web service description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1814">For more information about Visio for the web, see the [Visio for the web service description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md).</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1815"><sup>11</sup> 由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 即將推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1815"><sup>11</sup> Coming soon to Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1816"><sup>15</sup> Google 服務 (包括 Play 商店) 無法在中國記憶體取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1816"><sup>15</sup> Google services (including Play Store) are not accessible inside China.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1817">主要電話製造商或搜尋引擎公司會維護許多應用程式存放區，使用者可以從這裡安裝行動應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1817">There are several app stores maintained by major phone manufacturers or search engine companies that users can install mobile apps from.</span></span>

## <a name="office-for-the-web-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1818">網頁版 Office 的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1818">Office for the web features</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-1819">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-1819">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2642"><sup>3</sup> 郵件流程規則 (（也稱為傳輸規則) ）是由彈性準則所組成，可讓您根據準則定義要採取的條件、例外狀況和動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2642"><sup>3</sup> Mail flow rules (also known as transport rules) are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions, exceptions and actions to take based on the criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2643">Exchange Online 和 Microsoft Exchange Server 可用的條件、例外狀況和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2643">The available conditions, exceptions, and actions differ between Exchange Online and Microsoft Exchange Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2644">如需詳細資訊，請參閱各項產品的對應主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2644">For more information, see the corresponding topics for each product.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2645"><sup>4</sup> 只能透過直接存取 Exchange 系統管理中心 (EAC) 管理介面進行存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2645"><sup>4</sup> Only accessible via direct access to the Exchange admin center (EAC) management interface.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2646"><sup>5</sup> Exchange Server 2013 只會使用 Microsoft 反惡意程式碼引擎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2646"><sup>5</sup> Exchange Server 2013 uses only the Microsoft anti-malware engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2647">Exchange Online 使用多個反惡意程式碼引擎，來掃描輸入、輸出和內部訊息中是否有惡意程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2647">Exchange Online uses multiple anti-malware engines to scan inbound, outbound, and internal messages for malware.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2648"><sup>6</sup> 針對需要非使用中信箱功能的信箱，可另外購買 EOA 訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2648"><sup>6</sup> An EOA subscription can be purchased separately for each mailbox that requires the inactive mailbox feature.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2649"><sup>7</sup> 針對 eDiscovery，您需要針對內部部署與雲端使用個別查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2649"><sup>7</sup> For eDiscovery, you need a separate query for on-premises vs. cloud.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2650"><sup>8</sup> 支援 POP，但是不支援 IMAP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2650"><sup>8</sup> POP is supported, but IMAP is not.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2651"><sup>9</sup> Office 365 商務基本版和商務版，不會提供與內部部署伺服器的使用方式存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2651"><sup>9</sup> Office 365 Business Essentials and Business Premium do not provide access rights for utilization with on-premises servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2652">為了相容，客戶必須購買或已購買適當的 CAL，或升級至提供這些存取權的企業版 SKU。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2652">To be compliant, customer must purchase or have previously purchased the appropriate CALs or upgrade to an Enterprise SKU, which provides these access rights.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2653"><sup>10</sup> 混合式設定向導可用於 Exchange 2013 CU5 和較大的內部部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2653"><sup>10</sup> The Hybrid Configuration wizard is available for Exchange 2013 CU5 and greater on-premises deployments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2654">不過，有些混合式功能具有限制-請參閱 [說明] 主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2654">However, some hybrid features have limitations - see the help topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2655">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [由世紀運作的 Office 365](/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china?preserve-view=true&view=o365-21vianet)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2655">For details, see [Office 365 operated by 21Vianet](/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china?preserve-view=true&view=o365-21vianet).</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2656"><sup>11</sup> 對於由世紀運作的 Office 365，LinkedIn 可供使用，但不能使用 Facebook。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2656"><sup>11</sup> For Office 365 operated by 21Vianet, LinkedIn is available, but not Facebook.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2657"><sup>12</sup> 混合式部署設定可透過 exchange 2013 CU5 的混合式設定向導取得，如果您有 exchange 2013 SP1，也可以手動設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2657"><sup>12</sup> Hybrid deployment setup is available through the Hybrid Configuration wizard for Exchange 2013 CU5, or can be set up manually if you have Exchange 2013 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2658">如需詳細資訊，請參閱說明主題，請參閱 [由世紀運作的 Office 365](/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china?preserve-view=true&view=o365-21vianet)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2658">See the help topic For details, see [Office 365 operated by 21Vianet](/office365/admin/services-in-china/services-in-china?preserve-view=true&view=o365-21vianet).</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2659"><sup>13</sup> 已連線的帳戶支援 POP &amp; IMAP 帳戶，但對 Outlook.com (Hotmail) 停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2659"><sup>13</sup> Connected accounts are supported for POP &amp; IMAP accounts, but disabled for Outlook.com (Hotmail).</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2660"><sup>14</sup> 不支援使用 Cmdlet 來使用通訊清單及全域通訊清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2660"><sup>14</sup> Using a cmdlet to work with the Address List and Global Address List is not supported.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2661"><sup>15</sup> 目前的 Office 365 郵件加密 (OME) 功能是目前的資訊版權管理 (IRM) 和舊版的 OME 解決方案演變。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2661"><sup>15</sup> The current Office 365 Message Encryption (OME) capabilities are an evolution of the current Information Rights Management (IRM) and previous OME solutions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2662">如需 OME 的詳細資訊，請參閱 [Office 365 Message ENCRYPTION FAQ](/microsoft-365/compliance/ome-faq)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2662">For more information about OME, see [Office 365 Message Encryption FAQ](/microsoft-365/compliance/ome-faq).</span></span>

> - <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2680">Exchange Online Protection (EOP) 預設會保護 Exchange Online 信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2680">By default, Exchange Online Protection (EOP) protects Exchange Online mailboxes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2681">若要了解適用於 Exchange Online中 EOP 功能的限制，請參閱 [Exchange Online Protection 限制](../exchange-online-protection-service-description/exchange-online-protection-limits.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2681">For limits that apply to EOP features in Exchange Online, see [Exchange Online Protection limits](../exchange-online-protection-service-description/exchange-online-protection-limits.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2773"><sup>1</sup> 郵件使用者會定義為「信箱」，而且可以連同外部郵件連絡人直接在 Exchange 系統管理中心 (EAC) 中新增、移除或管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2773"><sup>1</sup> Mail users are defined as "Mailboxes," and, along with external mail contacts, can be added, removed, and otherwise managed directly in the Exchange admin center (EAC).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2774"><sup>2</sup> 沒有 RBAC 自訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2774"><sup>2</sup> No RBAC customization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2775">僅限系統管理員角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2775">Admin roles only.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2776"><sup>3</sup> 在 EAC 中，可檢視受管理網域和編輯網域類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2776"><sup>3</sup> Managed domains can be viewed and domain types can be edited in the EAC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2777">所有其他網域管理都必須在 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2777">All other domain management must be done in the Microsoft 365 admin center.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2778"><sup>4</sup> 郵件流程規則 (也稱為「傳輸規則」) 在 [Exchange Online Protection (傳輸規則) 中的郵件流程規則](/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0)中所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2778"><sup>4</sup> Mail flow rules (also known as transport rules) in EOP are described in [Mail flow rules (transport rules) in Exchange Online Protection](/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/mail-flow-rules-transport-rules-0).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2779">EOP 與 Exchange Online 之間的可用郵件流程規則條件、例外狀況和動作略有不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2779">The available mail flow rule conditions, exceptions, and actions differ slightly between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2780">在 exchange Online 中和[郵件流程規則動作的](/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions)[郵件流程規則條件和例外狀況) 中](/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions)，會記下這些差異 (述詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2780">These differences are noted in [Mail flow rule conditions and exceptions (predicates) in Exchange Online](/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/conditions-and-exceptions) and [Mail flow rule actions in Exchange Online](/Exchange/security-and-compliance/mail-flow-rules/mail-flow-rule-actions).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2781"><sup>5</sup> EOP 稽核報告是 Exchange Online 稽核報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2781"><sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2782"><sup>5</sup> EOP 稽核報告是 Exchange Online 稽核報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2782"><sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2783"><sup>6</sup> 預設的內容篩選動作，就是將垃圾郵件移至收件者的 [垃圾郵件] 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2783"><sup>6</sup> The default content filter action is to move spam messages to the recipients' Junk Email folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2784">若要使用內部部署 Exchange 信箱，您也需要在內部部署 Exchange 組織中設定兩個傳輸規則，以偵測 EOP 新增的垃圾郵件頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2784">For this to work with on-premises Exchange mailboxes, you also need to configure two transport rules in your on-premises Exchange organization to detect spam headers added by EOP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2785">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [確定垃圾郵件路由傳送至每個使用者的垃圾郵件資料夾](/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2785">For more information, see [Ensure that spam is routed to each user's Junk Email folder](/microsoft-365/security/office-365-security/ensure-that-spam-is-routed-to-each-user-s-junk-email-folder).</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2786"><sup>7</sup> 透過 EOP 篩選其信箱的 Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) 客戶可以使用此功能，而且很快就可以供 Exchange Online 客戶使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2786"><sup>7</sup> This feature is available to Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) customers whose mailboxes are being filtered by EOP, and will soon be available to Exchange Online customers.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2787"><sup>8</sup> EOP 報告是 Exchange Online 報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2787"><sup>8</sup> EOP reports are a subset of Exchange Online reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2788"><sup>9</sup> 包括 DLP 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2788"><sup>9</sup> Includes DLP reports.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2789"><sup>10</sup> 會掃描輸入及輸出郵件，但不掃描從組織中寄件者傳送給組織中收件者的內部郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2789"><sup>10</sup> Scans inbound and outbound messages, but does not scan internal messages sent from a sender in your organization to a recipient in your organization.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2790"><sup>11</sup> EOP 與 Exchange Online 可用的述詞和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2790"><sup>11</sup> The available predicates and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2791"><sup>12</sup> 混合式安裝程式不能透過混合式精靈使用，但您可以手動設定 (如果您有 Exchange SP1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2791"><sup>12</sup> Hybrid setup is not available through Hybrid Wizard, but can be set up manually if you have Exchange SP1.</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2792"><sup>13</sup> 目前的 Office 365 郵件加密 (OME) 功能是目前的資訊版權管理 (IRM) 和舊版的 OME 解決方案演變。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2792"><sup>13</sup> The current Office 365 Message Encryption (OME) capabilities are an evolution of the current Information Rights Management (IRM) and previous OME solutions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2793">如需 OME 的詳細資訊，請參閱 [Office 365 Message ENCRYPTION FAQ](/microsoft-365/compliance/ome-faq)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2793">For more information about OME, see [Office 365 Message Encryption FAQ](/microsoft-365/compliance/ome-faq).</span></span>

## <a name="exchange-online-archiving-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2794">Exchange Online 封存功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2794">Exchange Online Archiving features</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2796">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2796">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2799">**Exchange Server for Office 365 (21Vianet 運作的 Office 365) 的 Exchange Online 封存**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2799">**Exchange Online Archiving for Exchange Server for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2800">雲端型封存，適用於在 Exchange Server 2013 或 Exchange 2010 (SP2 或更新版本) 中有主要信箱的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2800">Cloud-based archive for users with primary mailboxes in Exchange Server 2013 or Exchange 2010 (SP2 or later).</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2801">如果您想要將雲端型封存新增至位於內部部署 Exchange 伺服器的主要信箱，您需要設定混合部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2801">If you want to add a cloud-based archive to a primary mailbox that's located on an on-premises Exchange server, you need to configure a hybrid deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2802">如需混合式部署的詳細資訊，請參閱 [Exchange Server 混合部署](/exchange/exchange-hybrid)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2802">For more information about hybrid deployments, see [Exchange Server Hybrid Deployments](/exchange/exchange-hybrid).</span></span>|

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2867"><sup>1</sup> 使用者信箱必須位於 Exchange 2010 SP2 或更新版本上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2867"><sup>1</sup> User mailboxes must reside on Exchange 2010 SP2 or later.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2868"><sup>2</sup> 「就地封存」僅可用來封存已套用授權之單一使用者或實體的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2868"><sup>2</sup> In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity for which a license has been applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2869">禁止使用「就地封存」來儲存多個使用者或實體的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2869">Using an In-Place Archive as a means to store mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2870">例如，IT 系統管理員無法建立共用信箱，並讓使用者透過 [ (副本] 或 [密件副本] 欄位，或是透過郵件流程規則) 共用信箱，以明確的封存目的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2870">For example, IT administrators can't create shared mailboxes and have users copy (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a mail flow rule) a shared mailbox for the explicit purpose of archiving.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2871"><sup>3</sup> 如需支援的 Microsoft Outlook 版本清單，請參閱 [Exchange Online 封存中的用戶端功能](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2871"><sup>3</sup> For a list of supported Microsoft Outlook versions see [Client features in Exchange Online Archiving](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2872"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2872"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-2873"><sup>5</sup> 當您對信箱進行就地保留或訴訟資料暫留時，會同時保留主要和封存信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-2873"><sup>5</sup> When you put a mailbox on In-Place Hold or Litigation Hold, the hold is placed on both the primary and the archive mailbox.</span></span>

## <a name="skype-for-business-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-4786">商務用 Skype Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-4786">Skype for Business Online features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="78c4a-4787">下表列出可用於由 21Vianet 方案運作之 Office 365 的 Exchange Online 保護 (EOP) 商務用 Skype Online 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-4787">The following table lists Skype for Business Online features that are available across Office 365 operated by 21Vianet plans.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-4788">此表格指出不同 Office 365 選項中的用戶端和服務可用性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-4788">This table indicates client and service availability across Office 365 options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-4789">如果您想要比較各商務用 Skype 桌面用戶端、網頁用戶端和行動用戶端之間的個別功能，請參閱 [桌面用戶端比較表](/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables) 及行動 [用戶端比較表](/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-mobile-client-comparison-tables)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-4789">If you want to compare individual features among the various Skype for Business desktop clients, web clients, and mobile clients, see [Desktop client comparison tables](/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-desktop-client-comparison-tables) and [Mobile Client Comparison Tables](/lyncserver/lync-server-2013-mobile-client-comparison-tables).</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="78c4a-4790">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-4790">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

## <a name="follow-on-wechat"></a><span data-ttu-id="78c4a-6626">在 WeChat 上關注我們</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="78c4a-6626">Follow on WeChat</span></span>
